Transition Advisory: Staff Communication Strategy for Integration As part of the integration plan between WestCoast Holdings and your firm, it is critical that communications to staff be transparent, timely, and empathetic. Avoid jargon such as “synergy” or “optimization” — employees respond better to clarity about job security and new reporting lines. Schedule a series of live Q&A sessions led by line managers, not just HR. Consider distributing a simple one-pager summarizing key dates and changes in both English and Spanish. Employees want to know how this affects them personally — not just the corporate narrative. Quiet resentment builds when silence replaces honesty.

Communication: Travel Policy Update Effective immediately, all employee travel must be pre-approved via the new HR Portal. This includes international trips, overnight stays, and reimbursable expenses. Please review the updated guidelines posted on the intranet under Employee Resources by Friday. Updated Guidelines for Business Travel Expenses We have revised our travel reimbursement protocol to align with fiscal year budget targets. All receipts must now be submitted within 7 calendar days of trip completion, regardless of location. Personal expenses such as spa services or premium lounge access are no longer eligible. Please ensure your manager approves your itinerary before booking. These changes take effect next Monday and are mandatory for all staff.
Important Changes to Remote Work and Travel Protocols As we transition into the new fiscal quarter, our team’s travel and remote work expectations have been adjusted. You are no longer permitted to combine personal leave with business travel without prior written authorization. All travel must be logged in the company’s new tracking system. This is not a suggestion — it’s a compliance requirement enforced by HR. If you need flexibility, submit a formal request to your department head.
